DROP TABLE Flights;

-- Drop the Maintenance_Parts table
DROP TABLE Maintenance_Parts;

-- Drop the Maintenance table
DROP TABLE Maintenance;

-- Drop the Airplanes table
DROP TABLE Airplanes;


-- Create the Airplanes table
CREATE TABLE Airplanes (
    airplane_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    model VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    capacity NUMBER NOT NULL CHECK (capacity > 0),
    manufacture_date DATE NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Maintenance table
CREATE TABLE Maintenance (
    maintenance_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    description VARCHAR2(30)
);

-- Create the Maintenance_Parts table
CREATE TABLE Maintenance_Parts (
    part_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    replacement_date DATE NOT NULL,
    cost NUMBER CHECK (cost >= 0),
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Flights table
CREATE TABLE Flights (
    flight_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    airplane_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Airplanes(airplane_id),
    flight_number VARCHAR2(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    departure_time DATE NOT NULL,
    arrival_time DATE NOT NULL,
    origin VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    destination VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT chk_flight_times CHECK (arrival_time > departure_time)
);

-- Create the Members table
CREATE TABLE Members (
    member_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR2(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    phone VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    address VARCHAR2(30),
    date_of_birth DATE NOT NULL,
    membership_date DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE,
    total_trips NUMBER DEFAULT 0
);

-- Create the Promotions table
CREATE TABLE Promotions (
    promotion_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    start_date DATE NOT NULL,
    end_date DATE NOT NULL,
    discount_percentage NUMBER CHECK (discount_percentage >= 0 AND discount_percentage <= 100),
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL,
    minimum_trips_required NUMBER DEFAULT 0 CHECK (minimum_trips_required >= 0),
    CONSTRAINT chk_promotion_dates CHECK (end_date >= start_date)
);

-- Create the Staff table
CREATE TABLE Staff (
    staff_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR2(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    phone VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    gender CHAR(1) CHECK (gender IN ('F', 'M', '-')),
    position VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    hire_date DATE NOT NULL,
    salary NUMBER CHECK (salary >= 0)
);

-- Create the Passengers table
CREATE TABLE Passengers (
    passenger_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    member_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Members(member_id),
    name VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    phone VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    gender CHAR(1) CHECK (gender IN ('F', 'M', '-')),
    passport_number VARCHAR2(30) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    nationality VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Maintenance_Tasks table
CREATE TABLE Maintenance_Tasks (
    maintenance_task_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    maintenance_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Maintenance(maintenance_id),
    airplane_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Airplanes(airplane_id),
    part_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Maintenance_Parts(part_id),
    maintenance_date DATE NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Workload_Allocations table
CREATE TABLE Workload_Allocations (
    allocation_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    staff_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Staff(staff_id),
    flight_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Flights(flight_id),
    role VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    allocation_date DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Bookings table
CREATE TABLE Bookings (
    booking_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    flight_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Flights(flight_id),
    passenger_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Passengers(passenger_id),
    booking_date DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
    seat_number VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL,
    payment_status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Luggage table
CREATE TABLE Luggage (
    luggage_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    booking_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Bookings(booking_id),
    weight NUMBER CHECK (weight >= 0),
    type VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    check_in_status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL,
    lost_status VARCHAR2(12),
    report_date DATE
);

-- Create the Insurance_Policies table
CREATE TABLE Insurance_Policies (
    policy_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    policy_type VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    coverage_amount NUMBER CHECK (coverage_amount >= 0),
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Items table
CREATE TABLE Items (
    item_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    type VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
    price NUMBER CHECK (price >= 0),
    availability_status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Item_Purchases table
CREATE TABLE Item_Purchases (
    purchase_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    booking_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Bookings(booking_id),
    item_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Items(item_id),
    purchase_date DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
    quantity NUMBER CHECK (quantity > 0)
);

-- Create the Promotion_Applications table
CREATE TABLE Promotion_Applications (
    application_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    promotion_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Promotions(promotion_id),
    booking_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Bookings(booking_id),
    application_date DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
    discount_amount NUMBER CHECK (discount_amount >= 0)
);

-- Create the Insurance_Claims table
CREATE TABLE Insurance_Claims (
    claim_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    policy_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Insurance_Policies(policy_id),
    booking_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Bookings(booking_id),
    claim_date DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
    amount NUMBER CHECK (amount >= 0),
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL
);

-- Create the Payments table
CREATE TABLE Payments (
    payment_id VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
    booking_id VARCHAR2(5) REFERENCES Bookings(booking_id),
    payment_date DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
    amount NUMBER CHECK (amount >= 0),
    payment_method VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR2(12) NOT NULL
);

-- Create a function to generate random IDs
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION generate_random_id (p_length IN NUMBER) RETURN VARCHAR2 IS
    v_random_id VARCHAR2(32767);
BEGIN
    SELECT DBMS_RANDOM.STRING('X', p_length) INTO v_random_id FROM dual;
    RETURN v_random_id;
END;
/

-- Table summary
-- Count of rows in Airplanes table
SELECT 'Airplanes' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Airplanes;

-- Count of rows in Maintenance table
SELECT 'Maintenance' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Maintenance;

-- Count of rows in Maintenance_Parts table
SELECT 'Maintenance_Parts' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Maintenance_Parts;

-- Count of rows in Flights table
SELECT 'Flights' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Flights;

-- Count of rows in Members table
SELECT 'Members' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Members;

-- Count of rows in Promotions table
SELECT 'Promotions' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Promotions;

-- Count of rows in Staff table
SELECT 'Staff' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Staff;

-- Count of rows in Passengers table
SELECT 'Passengers' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Passengers;

-- Count of rows in Maintenance_Tasks table
SELECT 'Maintenance_Tasks' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Maintenance_Tasks;

-- Count of rows in Workload_Allocations table
SELECT 'Workload_Allocations' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Workload_Allocations;

-- Count of rows in Bookings table
SELECT 'Bookings' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Bookings;

-- Count of rows in Luggage table
SELECT 'Luggage' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Luggage;

-- Count of rows in Insurance_Policies table
SELECT 'Insurance_Policies' AS table_name, COUNT(*) AS total_rows FROM Insurance_Policies;
